		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	# Ok
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0076.a
		add_piety = 50
		add_prestige = -50
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { var:RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_cave_size = 4 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_cave_size
				add = 1
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0076.a.tooltip
	}
	
	# Give them donations instead
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0076.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 50
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 50
		add_piety = 100
		add_prestige = 50
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	# Don't need their help
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0076.c
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Conflict with merchants building their own cave nearby
tarim_basin.0078 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0078.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0078.desc
	theme = corruption
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_dunhuang_mogao_caves }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = anger
	}
	
	# Back off, don't fight
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0078.a
		add_prestige = -50
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	# Pay them to screw off
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0078.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 25
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	# Forget the merchants!
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0078.c
		add_piety = -50
		stress_impact = {
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
			calm = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	# Perhaps we can combine our caves
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0078.d
		trigger = {
			diplomacy >= medium_skill_rating		
		}
		skill = diplomacy
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = medium_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { var:RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_cave_size = 4 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_cave_size
				add = 1
			}
		}
		trigger_event = tarim_basin.0079
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0078.d.tooltip
	}
}

# You befriend one of the merchants who offers to join your court
tarim_basin.0080 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0080.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0080.desc
	theme = RICE_theme_dunhuang_villa
	override_icon = { reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_duty.dds" }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = happiness
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:merchant
		animation = throne_room_bow_2
	}

	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = mogao_cave_merchant_template
			save_scope_as = merchant
			culture = root.culture
			faith = root.faith
		}
	}
	
	# Ok
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0080.a
		add_courtier = scope:merchant
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_set_relation_friend_trigger = { CHARACTER = scope:merchant }
			}
			set_relation_friend = {
				target = scope:merchant
				reason = RICE_friend_reason_placeholder
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:merchant
					type = loyalty_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:merchant
				type = loyalty_hook
			}
		}
	}
}

			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

				}
				create_character = {
					location = root.location
					template = mogao_cave_foreign_artist_template
					save_scope_as = foreigner
					culture = culture:uyghur
					faith = root.faith
				}				
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Not my problem
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0082.a
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:foreigner = {		
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Help them with misunderstandings
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0082.b
		add_prestige = -25
		add_piety = 25
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					trigger_event = tarim_basin.0083
				}
				# He disappears
				80 = {
					scope:foreigner = {		
						death = {
							death_reason = death_disappearance
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Make preparations to begin the pilgrimage
tarim_basin.0090 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0090.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0090.desc
	theme = travel_pilgrimage
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_tarim_basin_landscape }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		is_available_travelling = yes
		is_landed = yes
		exists = involved_activity
		involved_activity = {
			has_activity_type = activity_RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_pilgrimage
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		faith = {
			save_scope_as = faith
		}
		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0090.a
	}
}

# Prepare to stage an animal fight
tarim_basin.0100 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0100.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0100.desc
	theme = realm
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_tarim_basin_town }
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	immediate = {
		capital_province = { save_scope_as = capital_province } #For loc.
		# Stop characters from planning multiple activities at once.
		# add_character_flag = planning_an_activity

		# If you are Tocharian yourself
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tocharian }
			}
			culture = {
				save_scope_as = culture_scope
			}
		}
		# Save your county's culture if you are not Tocharian, as it is presumably TOcharian
		else = {
			capital_county = {
				culture = { save_scope_as = culture_scope }
			}			
		}


	}
	
	option = { # Cattle
		name = tarim_basin.0100.a
		trigger = {
			scope:activity = {
				has_activity_option = {
					category = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type
					option = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type_cattle
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.a.tooltip
		set_variable = {
			name = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal
			value = flag:cattle
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.tooltip
	}
	
	option = { # Horses
		name = tarim_basin.0100.b
		trigger = {
			scope:activity = {
				has_activity_option = {
					category = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type
					option = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type_horses
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.b.tooltip
		set_variable = {
			name = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal
			value = flag:horses
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.tooltip
	}
	
	option = { # Camels
		name = tarim_basin.0100.c
		trigger = {
			scope:activity = {
				has_activity_option = {
					category = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type
					option = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type_camels
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.c.tooltip
		set_variable = {
			name = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal
			value = flag:camels
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.tooltip
	}
	
	option = { # Goats
		name = tarim_basin.0100.d
		trigger = {
			scope:activity = {
				has_activity_option = {
					category = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type
					option = RICE_tocharian_animal_fight_type_goats
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.d.tooltip
		set_variable = {
			name = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal
			value = flag:goats
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0100.tooltip
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0101
			days = { 3 9 }
		}
	}

}


# Animal Fight starts
tarim_basin.0101 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0101.t
	desc = {
		desc = tarim_basin.0101.desc.intro
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:cattle
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0101.desc.cattle
			}	
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:horses
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0101.desc.horses
			}	
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:camels
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0101.desc.camels
			}	
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:goats
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0101.desc.goats
			}	
		}
		desc = tarim_basin.0101.desc.conclusion
	}
	theme = tournament_grounds
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_banquet
		capital_province = { save_scope_as = capital_province } #For loc.
		
		# If you are Tocharian yourself
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tocharian }
			}
			culture = {
				save_scope_as = culture_scope
			}
		}
		# Save your county's culture if you are not Tocharian, as it is presumably TOcharian
		else = {
			capital_county = {
				culture = { save_scope_as = culture_scope }
			}			
		}

	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0101.a
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0102
			days = 7
		}
	}
}

					limit = {
						root = {
							var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:cattle
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = {
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_cattle_good_character
								years = 7
							}
						}
						33 = {
							capital_county = {
								add_county_modifier = {
									modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_cattle_good_county
									years = 7
								}			
							} 
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:horses
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = {
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_horses_good_character
								years = 7
							}
						}
						33 = {
							capital_county = {
								add_county_modifier = {
									modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_horses_good_county

								}			
							} 
						}
					}	
				}
			}
			20 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_result
					value = flag:great
				}
				add_prestige = 150
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:cattle
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = {
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_cattle_great_character
								years = 7
							}
						}
						33 = {
							capital_county = {
								add_county_modifier = {
									modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_cattle_great_county
									years = 7
								}			
							} 
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:horses
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = {
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_horses_great_character
								years = 7
							}
						}
						33 = {
							capital_county = {
								add_county_modifier = {
									modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_horses_great_county
									years = 7
								}			
							} 
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:camels
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = {
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_camels_great_character
								years = 7
							}
						}
						33 = {
							capital_county = {
								add_county_modifier = {
									modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_camels_great_county
									years = 7
								}			
							} 
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							var:RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal = flag:goats
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = {
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_goats_great_character
								years = 7
							}
						}
						33 = {
							capital_county = {
								add_county_modifier = {
									modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fight_goats_great_county
									years = 7
								}			
							} 
						}
					}	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0102.a
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal }
			remove_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_tocharian_fight_animal
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:activity = {
				hidden_effect = { skip_activity_phase = yes }
			}
		}
	}

}

# Procession starts
tarim_basin.0152 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0152.t
	desc = {
		desc = tarim_basin.0152.desc.intro
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					has_title = title:c_khotan
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0152.desc.khotan_ruler
			}	
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { has_title = title:c_khotan }
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0152.desc.not_khotan_ruler
			}
		}
	}
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_tarim_basin_landscape }

	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:khotan_ruler
		animation = personality_honorable		
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:khotan_ruler
			NOT = {
				root = {
					has_title = title:c_khotan
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = throne_room_bow_1
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0152.a
		# Reflect on one of the Khotanese Buddhist legends
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					# Nothing
				}
				# Eight Protector kings
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0154
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Deer of Saṃjñāya - founding of Gomati
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0155
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Princess Vimalaprabha Khotan legends
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0156
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Buddha drains the lake
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0157
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Ashoka’s son, adopted by Chinese king
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0158
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Story about the Silk Princess
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0159
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Hill of Gautośan, with the monastery of Kāśyapa relics
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0160
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
				# Miraculous statue of Pimo
				10 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0161
						days = { 3 11 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0153
			days = 14
		}
	}

}

######################################################################################
# 
# EIGHT PROTECTORS
# 
# tarim_basin.0170-tarim_basin.0199

######################################################################################


# Change Khotan's Eight Protectors ruler modifier (for title transition)
tarim_basin.0170 = {
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		scope:title = title:c_khotan
		NOT = { has_global_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors_abandoned }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = religion:buddhism_religion
				scope:previous_holder = { 
					is_alive = yes
					has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors
					NOT = {
						has_title = title:c_khotan
					}
				}
			}
			scope:previous_holder = { remove_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors }
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_remain_trigger = no
				NOT = {
					any_liege_or_above = {
						RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_remain_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = khotan_new_ruler
			scope:khotan_new_ruler = {
				add_to_global_variable_list = {
					name = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_non_buddhist_maker_list # Dunno how else to do this
					target = this
				}	
			}
			RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_abandoned_effect = yes
			every_player = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
					any_held_title = {
						tier = tier_county
						any_county_province = {
							geographical_region = RICE_land_silk_road_region
						}
					}	
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0172
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Change Khotan's Eight Protectors ruler modifier (for religious conversion)
tarim_basin.0171 = {
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_title = title:c_khotan
		NOT = { has_global_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors_abandoned }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Lose it if you convert away from Buddhism
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = religion:buddhism_religion }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors
			if = {
				limit = {
					RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_remain_trigger = no
					NOT = {
						any_liege_or_above = {
							RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_remain_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = khotan_new_ruler
				scope:khotan_new_ruler = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = {
						name = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_non_buddhist_maker_list # Dunno how else to do this
						target = this
					}	
				}
				RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_abandoned_effect = yes
				every_player = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = no
						any_held_title = {
							tier = tier_county
							any_county_province = {
								geographical_region = RICE_land_silk_road_region
							}
						}	
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = tarim_basin.0172
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# Gain it if you convert away to Buddhism
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = religion:buddhism_religion
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors
			}
		}
	}
}



# Khotan is ruled by someone unfriendly to Buddhists, and the monks flee
tarim_basin.0172 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0172.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0172.desc
	theme = faith
	#override_background = { reference = burning_building }

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:khotan_new_ruler
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_sacredrite"
		title:c_khotan = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = khotan
		}
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:khotan_new_ruler = {
				RICE_tarim_basin_eight_protectors_abandoned_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	# Ok
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0172.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion = religion:buddhism_religion }
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0172.tooltip.1
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0172.tooltip.2
	}
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0172.b
		trigger = {
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0172.tooltip.1
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0172.tooltip.2
	}

}


# Khotanese refugees arrive at a Buddhist ruler's court
tarim_basin.0173 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0173.t
	desc = {
		desc = tarim_basin.0173.desc
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					scope:khotan_refugee = {
						has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_monastic_refugee
					}
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0173.desc.monastic
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					scope:khotan_refugee = {
						has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_noble_refugee
					}
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0173.desc.noble
			}
		}
	}
	theme = realm

	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:khotan_refugee
		animation = beg
	}
	lower_center_portrait = scope:khotan_new_ruler

	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_eight_protectors_abandoned
	}

	immediate = {
		title:c_khotan = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = khotan
		}
		ordered_in_global_list = {
			variable = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_non_buddhist_maker_list
			save_scope_as = khotan_new_ruler
		}
		random_list = {
			# Get a monastic
			66 = {
				create_character = {
					location = root.location
					template = RICE_khotan_refugee_monk_template
					save_scope_as = khotan_refugee
					culture = scope:khotan.culture
					faith = root.faith
				}
			}
			# Get a noble
			33 = {
				create_character = {
					location = root.location
					template = RICE_khotan_refugee_noble_template
					save_scope_as = khotan_refugee
					culture = scope:khotan.culture
					faith = root.faith
				}				
			}
		}
	}

	# Welcome Them
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0173.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 40
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 40
		add_piety = 50
		add_courtier = scope:khotan_refugee
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:khotan_refugee = {
					has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_monastic_refugee
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_helped_khotan_monastic_refugees
				years = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:khotan_refugee = {
					has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_khotan_noble_refugee
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_helped_khotan_noble_refugees
				years = 10
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}
	# No
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0173.b
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:khotan_refugee = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}


# Reinhabit Gomati Monastery
tarim_basin.0174 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0174.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0174.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_tarim_basin_town }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:khotan_buddhism_restorer
		animation = personality_zealous
	}

	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"
		title:c_khotan = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = khotan
		}
		RICE_tarim_basin_reinhabit_gomati_monastery_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0174.a
		every_ruler = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				#OR = {
					any_held_title = {
						tier = tier_county
						any_county_province = {
							geographical_region = RICE_silk_road_region
						}
					}
				#	dynasty = root.dynasty # Shows errors for some reason?
				#}
			}
			trigger_event = tarim_basin.0175
		}	
	}
}

		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:khotan_buddhism_restorer = {
				RICE_tarim_basin_reinhabit_gomati_monastery_effect = yes
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok

		}

		}

# First Muslim ruler of Khotan
tarim_basin.0176 = {
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent_happened }
		has_title = title:c_khotan
		religion = religion:islam_religion
		game_start_date < 1000.1.1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = {
			name = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent_happened
			value = yes 
		}
		#RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent_died
		save_scope_as = ali_arslan
		scope:ali_arslan = {
			add_to_global_variable_list = {
				name = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent # Dunno how else to do this
				target = this
			}	
		}
		add_piety_level = 1		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent
		}
		every_player = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				religion = religion:islam_religion
				any_held_title = {
					tier = tier_county
					any_county_province = {
						geographical_region = RICE_former_tang_western_region
					}
				}		
			}
			
			trigger_event = {
				id = tarim_basin.0177
				days = 1
			}
			
		}
	}
}

# First Muslim ruler of Khotan passes away ping
tarim_basin.0178 = {
	scope = none
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent
	}
	
	immediate = {
		religion:islam_religion = { save_scope_as = islam_religion }
		title:c_kashgar = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = kashgar
		}
		title:c_khotan = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = khotan
		}
		#save_scope_as = ali_arslan
		ordered_in_global_list = {
			variable = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent
			save_scope_as = ali_arslan
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent_died
			value = yes 
		}
		every_player = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				any_held_title = {
					tier = tier_county
					any_county_province = {
						geographical_region = RICE_former_tang_western_region
					}
				}		
			}
			trigger_event = tarim_basin.0179
		}
	}
}

# al-Kashgari introduction
tarim_basin.0200 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0200.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0200.desc
	theme = RICE_theme_tarim_basin_town
	override_icon = { reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_learning.dds" }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = war_defender
	}

	immediate = {
		show_as_tooltip = {			
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_is_al_kashgari
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0200.tooltip
		custom_description_no_bullet = {
			text = tarim_basin.0200.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0200.a
	}
}



# Start to Compile the Turkic Dictionary
tarim_basin.0201 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0201.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0201.desc
	theme = learning
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	immediate = {
		culture:turkish = {
			save_scope_as = culture_scope
		}
		show_as_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_working_on_turkic_dictionary
			}
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_gain
				lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # OK
		name = tarim_basin.0201.a
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0202
			days = { 365 1095 }
		}
	}
}



# Finish writing the Turkic Dictionary
tarim_basin.0202 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0202.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0202.desc
	theme = learning
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = happiness
	}

	artifact = { # To display the artifact in the event-window
		target = scope:turkic_dictionary
		position = lower_center_portrait
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_scope_as = compiler

		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"

		remove_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_working_on_turkic_dictionary


		if = {
			limit = {
				var:RICE_historical_aspiration ?= flag:al_kashgari
			}
			add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_al_kashgari_aspiration_done
		}
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_wrote_first_turkic_dictionary	
		}

		hidden_effect_new_object = {
			#set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes
			create_artifact = {
				name = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_name
				description = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_desc
				type = journal
				visuals = RICE_book_placeholder					
				quality = 80
				wealth = 80
				modifier = artifact_learn_language_scheme_phase_duration_add_2_modifier
				save_scope_as = turkic_dictionary
			}
			scope:turkic_dictionary = {
				add_artifact_modifier = artifact_diplomacy_1_modifier
				add_artifact_modifier = artifact_diplomacy_1_modifier
				add_artifact_modifier = artifact_learning_1_modifier
				add_artifact_modifier = artifact_learning_1_modifier
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
			}
			liege = {
				save_scope_as = liege
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				liege = {
					is_independent_ruler = no
				}
			}
			top_liege = {
				save_scope_as = top_liege
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = { exists = religious_head }
				any_held_title = { is_head_of_faith = no }
			}
			faith.religious_head = {
				save_scope_as = religious_head
			}
		}

	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0202.a
		add_prestige = 400
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:turkic_dictionary = {
				set_owner = {
					target = root
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				exists = liege
			}
			custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0202.copy.liege
			liege = {
				trigger_event = tarim_basin.0203	
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				liege = {
					is_independent_ruler = no
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0202.copy.top_liege
			top_liege = {
				trigger_event = tarim_basin.0203	
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = { exists = religious_head }
				any_held_title = { is_head_of_faith = no }
			}
			custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0202.copy.religious_head
			faith.religious_head = {
				trigger_event = tarim_basin.0203	
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_player = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_turkic }
				OR = {
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = language_turkic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = language_oghur }
				}	
			}
			add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:liege
			}
			scope:liege = {
				add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
				add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:top_liege
			}
			scope:top_liege = {
				add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
				add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:religious_head
			}
			scope:religious_head = {
				add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
				add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
		}
		every_in_list = {
			list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
			trigger_event = tarim_basin.0203
		}
	}

}



# Notification / Important people receive copies
tarim_basin.0203 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0203.t
	desc = {
		desc = tarim_basin.0203.desc
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0203.desc.copy
			}
		}
	}
	theme = learning
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:compiler
		animation = personality_content
	}

	artifact = { # To display the artifact in the event-window
		target = scope:turkic_dictionary
		position = lower_center_portrait
	}
	
	immediate = {

		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
			hidden_effect_new_object = {
				#set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes
				create_artifact = {
					name = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_name
					description = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_desc
					type = journal
					visuals = RICE_book_placeholder					
					quality = 80
					wealth = 80
					modifier = artifact_learn_language_scheme_phase_duration_add_2_modifier
					save_scope_as = turkic_dictionary
				}
				scope:turkic_dictionary = {
					add_artifact_modifier = artifact_diplomacy_1_modifier
					add_artifact_modifier = artifact_diplomacy_1_modifier
					add_artifact_modifier = artifact_learning_1_modifier
					add_artifact_modifier = artifact_learning_1_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0203.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
			show_as_tooltip = {
				scope:turkic_dictionary = {
					set_owner = {
						target = root
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
			remove_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
		}
	}

}


# Character dies before completing the Turkic dictionary
tarim_basin.0204 = {
	scope = none
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_target_in_global_variable_list = {
			name = unavailable_unique_decisions
			target = flag:RICE_tarim_basin_compile_turkic_dictionary_done
		}
		has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_working_on_turkic_dictionary
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_scope_as = compiler
		culture:turkish = {
			save_scope_as = culture_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = primary_heir
			}
			primary_heir = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0205
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		# If heir doesn't exist for some reason, quietly re-enable it
		else = {
			remove_list_global_variable = {
				name = unavailable_unique_decisions
				target = flag:RICE_tarim_basin_compile_turkic_dictionary_done
			}
		}
	}
}




# Finish writing the Turkic Dictionary (compiler passed away version)
tarim_basin.0205 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0205.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0205.desc
	theme = learning
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:compiler
		animation = personality_content
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	artifact = { # To display the artifact in the event-window
		target = scope:turkic_dictionary
		position = lower_center_portrait
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_scope_as = compiler_heir

		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"

		remove_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_working_on_turkic_dictionary

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_wrote_first_turkic_dictionary
			years = 10	
		}

		hidden_effect_new_object = {
			#set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes
			create_artifact = {
				name = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_name
				description = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_desc
				type = journal
				visuals = RICE_book_placeholder					
				quality = 40
				wealth = 40
				modifier = artifact_learn_language_scheme_phase_duration_add_1_modifier
				save_scope_as = turkic_dictionary
			}
			scope:turkic_dictionary = {
				add_artifact_modifier = artifact_diplomacy_1_modifier
				add_artifact_modifier = artifact_learning_1_modifier
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				exists = liege
			}
			liege = {
				save_scope_as = liege
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				liege = {
					is_independent_ruler = no
				}
			}
			top_liege = {
				save_scope_as = top_liege
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = { exists = religious_head }
				any_held_title = { is_head_of_faith = no }
			}
			faith.religious_head = {
				save_scope_as = liege
			}
		}

	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0205.a
		add_prestige = 100
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:turkic_dictionary = {
				set_owner = {
					target = root
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				exists = liege
			}
			custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0202.copy.liege
			liege = {
				trigger_event = tarim_basin.0206	
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_independent_ruler = no
				liege = {
					is_independent_ruler = no
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0202.copy.top_liege
			top_liege = {
				trigger_event = tarim_basin.0206	
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:compiler.faith = { exists = religious_head }
				any_held_title = { is_head_of_faith = no }
			}
			custom_tooltip = tarim_basin.0202.copy.religious_head
			scope:compiler.faith.religious_head = {
				trigger_event = tarim_basin.0206	
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_player = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_turkic }
				OR = {
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = language_turkic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = language_oghur }
				}	
			}
			add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:liege
			}
			scope:liege = {
				add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
				add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:top_liege
			}
			scope:top_liege = {
				add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
				add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:religious_head
			}
			scope:religious_head = {
				add_to_list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
				add_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
		}
		every_in_list = {
			list = turkic_dictionary_notification_list
			trigger_event = tarim_basin.0206
		}
	}

}

	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0206.t
	desc = {
		desc = tarim_basin.0206.desc
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
				}
				desc = tarim_basin.0206.desc.copy
			}
		}
	}
	theme = learning
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:compiler
		animation = personality_content
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:compiler_heir
		animation = admiration
	}

	artifact = { # To display the artifact in the event-window
		target = scope:turkic_dictionary
		position = lower_center_portrait
	}
	
	immediate = {

		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
			hidden_effect_new_object = {
				#set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes
				create_artifact = {
					name = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_name
					description = RICE_tarim_basin_first_turkic_dictionary_desc
					type = journal
					visuals = RICE_book_placeholder					
					quality = 40
					wealth = 40
					modifier = artifact_learn_language_scheme_phase_duration_add_1_modifier
					save_scope_as = turkic_dictionary
				}
				scope:turkic_dictionary = {
					add_artifact_modifier = artifact_diplomacy_1_modifier
					add_artifact_modifier = artifact_learning_1_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0206.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
			show_as_tooltip = {
				scope:turkic_dictionary = {
					set_owner = {
						target = root
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
			}
			remove_character_flag = RICE_tarim_basin_received_turkic_dictionary_copy
		}
	}

}

# Al-Kashgari dies
tarim_basin.0207 = {
	scope = none
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			is_target_in_global_variable_list = {
				name = unavailable_unique_decisions
				target = flag:RICE_tarim_basin_compile_turkic_dictionary_done
			}
		}
		has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_is_al_kashgari
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Enable it for anyone now that Al-Kashgari has passed away
		set_global_variable = {
			name = RICE_anyone_can_write_turkic_dictionary
			value = yes
		}
	}
}



# Al-Kashgari's Aspiration Fulfilled
tarim_basin.0208 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0208.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0208.desc
	theme = learning

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = war_over_win
	}

	immediate = {

		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"

		RICE_historical_aspiration_fulfilled_effect = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_is_al_kashgari
				}
				remove_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_is_al_kashgari
			}
		}

		# Main Objective Reward

		add_prestige = RICE_aspiration_medium_resource_bonus
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_is_al_kashgari_upgrade
		}

		# Bonus Objective Reward(s)
		# Know at least three languages
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_known_languages >= 3
			}
			add_relevant_lifestyle_perk_point_effect = { NUMBER = 1 }
		}

		# Have at least 3 prestige level/level of fame
		if = {
			limit = {
				prestige_level >= 3
			}
			add_diplomacy_skill = 1
			add_learning_skill = 1
		}

	}

	# Ok
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0208.a
	}


	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_caves_done_once }
			remove_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_mogao_caves_done_once
		}
	}

}

# Prepare for Ordam Mazar
tarim_basin.0210 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0210.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0210.desc
	theme = travel
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_content
	}

	lower_center_portrait = scope:ali_arslan

	trigger = {
		is_available_travelling = yes
		is_landed = yes
		exists = involved_activity	
		involved_activity = {
			has_activity_type = activity_RICE_tarim_basin_ordam_mazar
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent_died
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = {
				variable = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent
				save_scope_as = ali_arslan
			}
		}
		else = {
			character:3000 = {
				save_scope_as = ali_arslan
			}
		}
		title:c_kashgar = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = kashgar
		}
		title:c_khotan = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = khotan
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0210.a
	}
}

# Ordam Mazar begins
tarim_basin.0211 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0211.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0211.desc
	theme = realm
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_tarim_basin_town }
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:ali_arslan
		animation = personality_zealous
	}

	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_sacredrite"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_variable = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent_died
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = {
				variable = RICE_tarim_basin_ali_arslan_equivalent
				save_scope_as = ali_arslan
			}
		}
		else = {
			character:3000 = {
				save_scope_as = ali_arslan
			}
		}
		title:c_kashgar = { #For loc.
			save_scope_as = kashgar
		}

		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok

		trigger = {
			has_activity_intent = RICE_tarim_basin_ordam_mazar_remembrance_intent
		}
		add_piety = 25
		# stress_impact = {
		# 	cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		# 	gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain

	}

		# 	shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		# }
	}

	after = {

		# Random events

		hidden_effect = {
			# Singers and poets
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0215
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Women praying for children
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0216
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Old men dancing
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0217
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Young people gather to mingle and find partners
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0218
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Legends about Ali Arslan
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0219
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Legends about Ali Arslan's mom
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0220
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Food stalls at Ordam
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0221
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Light-hearted atmosphere at Ordam
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0222
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Mourning pilgrims
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0223
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Chatting with a peddler during Ordam
			random = {
				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0224
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
			# Meet people going on a pilgrimage tour
			random = {

					id = tarim_basin.0225
					days = { 3 18 }
				}

				chance = 15
				trigger_event = {
					id = tarim_basin.0226
					days = { 3 18 }
				}			
			}
		}




		# In real life it's just a few days, but we spread it out so there's a chance multiple events can trigger
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0212
			days = { 9 12 }
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0213
			days = { 20 25 }
		}
	}
}

# Become fake China
tarim_basin.0240 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0240.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0240.desc
	theme = crown
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = war_defender
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0240.a
		RICE_tarim_basin_claim_fake_china_effect = yes
		every_ruler = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				#OR = {
					any_held_title = {
						tier = tier_county
						any_county_province = {
							geographical_region = RICE_silk_road_region
						}
					}
				#	dynasty = root.dynasty # Shows errors for some reason?
				#}
			}
			trigger_event = tarim_basin.0241
		}	
	}
}

# Become fake China notification

	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0241.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0241.desc

		}
	}

		name = tarim_basin.0241.a	
	}
}




# Lose fake China status
tarim_basin.0242 = {
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_target_in_global_variable_list = {
			name = unavailable_unique_decisions
			target = flag:RICE_tarim_basin_fake_china_proclaimed_flag
		}
		exists = dynasty
		root.dynasty = {
			has_dynasty_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fake_china_dynasty
		}
		NOT = {
			root.dynasty = {
				any_dynasty_member = {
					is_landed = yes
					any_held_title = {
						tier = tier_county
						any_county_province = {
							geographical_region = RICE_former_tang_western_region	
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_scope_as = RICE_tarim_basin_fake_china_person
		dynasty = {
			remove_dynasty_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_fake_china_dynasty
		}
		every_ruler = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				#OR = {
					any_held_title = {
						tier = tier_county
						any_county_province = {
							geographical_region = RICE_silk_road_region
						}
					}
				#	dynasty = root.dynasty # Shows errors for some reason?
				#}
			}
			trigger_event = tarim_basin.0243
		}		
	}
}

# Yelu Yixin Aspiration Fulfilled
tarim_basin.0247 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0247.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0247.desc
	theme = RICE_theme_dunhuang_villa

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:yixin
		animation = scheme
	}
	lower_left_portrait = scope:daozong
	lower_right_portrait = scope:guanyin

	immediate = {

		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"

		RICE_historical_aspiration_fulfilled_effect = yes

		character:RICE_khitan_misc_001 = {
			save_scope_as = yixin
		}
		character:RICE_khitan_misc_003 = {
			save_scope_as = guanyin
		}
		title:e_great_liao.holder = {
			save_scope_as = daozong
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_aspiration_corrupt_liao_official
				}
				remove_character_modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_aspiration_corrupt_liao_official
			}
		}

		# Main Objective Reward
		add_diplomacy_lifestyle_perk_points = 1
		add_intrigue_lifestyle_perk_points = 1
		add_prestige = RICE_aspiration_large_resource_bonus
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = education_intrigue_4
			}
			remove_trait = education_intrigue_4
			add_trait_force_tooltip = education_intrigue_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:yixin = {
					can_add_hook = {
						target = scope:daozong
						type = RICE_tarim_basin_yelu_yixin_hook
					}
				}
			}
			scope:yixin = {
				add_hook = {
					target = scope:daozong
					type = RICE_tarim_basin_yelu_yixin_hook
				}
			}
		}

		# Bonus Objective Reward(s)
		if = {
			limit = {
				character:RICE_khitan_misc_003 = {
					exists = killer
					killer = root
				}
			}
			add_intrigue_lifestyle_perk_points = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				dread >= high_dread
			}
			spawn_army = {
				levies = 300
				men_at_arms = {
					type = pikemen_unit
					stacks = 1
				}
				men_at_arms = {
					type = armored_footmen
					stacks = 1
				}
				men_at_arms = {
					type = chu_ko_nu
					stacks = 1
				}
				men_at_arms = {
					type = cataphract_archers
					stacks = 1
				}
				men_at_arms = {
					type = RICE_iron_forest
					stacks = 1
				}
				men_at_arms = {
					type = nomad_lancers
					stacks = 1
				}
				men_at_arms = {
					type = steppe_raiders
					stacks = 2
				}
				location = root.capital_province
				uses_supply = yes
				inheritable = yes
				name = RICE_yelu_yixin_event_troops
			}
		}


	}

	# Ok
	option = {
		name = tarim_basin.0247.a
	}


}

			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2

		}
		modifier = {

		}
	}

		add_gold = 25
		add_piety = -50

			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain

			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Settle it in court

		add_gold = 25
		add_prestige = -50
		stress_impact = {
			impatient = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Come to an agreement
		name = tarim_basin.0255.d
		trigger = {
			diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
		}
		skill = diplomacy
		add_gold = 25
	}

		name = tarim_basin.0257.b

			custom = RICE_tarim_basin_every_buddhist_county
			limit = {
				tier = tier_county
				religion = religion:buddhism_religion
			}
			add_county_modifier = {
				modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_lax_monastic_regulations
				years = 10
			}	
		}
		stress_impact = {
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Dispute between Khotanese monk and Sogdian merchant

	type = character_event

	desc = tarim_basin.0261.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	trigger = {
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			any_county_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
					geographical_region = RICE_dunhuang_region
				}	
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = tarim_basin.0261.a
		add_prestige = 25
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = tarim_basin.0261.b
		add_piety = 25
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = tarim_basin.0261.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = diligent
			}
			stress_impact = {
				diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}		
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = tarim_basin.0261.d
		trigger = {
			stewardship >= decent_skill_rating
		}
		skill = stewardship
		add_prestige = 25
		add_piety = 25
	}
}

# PILGRIMAGE TO BEZEKLIK CAVES
# tarim_basin.0280-0089 reserved
# 
##################################################################

# Make preparations to begin the pilgrimage
tarim_basin.0280 = {
	type = character_event
	title = tarim_basin.0280.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0280.desc
	theme = travel_pilgrimage
	override_background = { reference = RICE_background_tarim_basin_landscape }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		is_available_travelling = yes
		is_landed = yes
		exists = involved_activity
		involved_activity = {
			has_activity_type = activity_RICE_tarim_basin_bezeklik_pilgrimage
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		faith = {
			save_scope_as = faith
		}
		play_music_cue = "mx_cue_epic_sacral_moment"
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0280.a
	}
}



# Arrive in Bezeklik
tarim_basin.0281 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0281.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0281.desc
	theme = RICE_theme_tarim_basin_town
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = holding_staff
	}

	immediate = {
		title:b_bezeklik = {
			save_scope_as = bezeklik
		}
		faith = {
			save_scope_as = faith
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0281.a
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0282
			days = { 3 8 }
		}
	}
}


# Pray at the caves
tarim_basin.0282 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0282.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0282.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = fp3_cave }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = prayer
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0282.a
		random = {
			chance = RICE_normandy_mont_saint_michel_chance
			scope:activity = {
				add_activity_log_entry = {
					key = RICE_tarim_basin_bezeklik_cave_pilgrimage_inspired_log
					tags = { good }
					# this line below adds the entry to the Effects section of the conclusion UI
					show_in_conclusion = yes
					character = scope:host
					scope:host = {	
						add_character_modifier = {
							modifier = RICE_tarim_basin_bezeklik_cave_pilgrimage_inspired
							years = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {		
		trigger_event = {
			id = tarim_basin.0283
			days = { 3 8 }
		}
	}

}


# Pilgrimage concludes
tarim_basin.0283 = {
	type = activity_event
	title = tarim_basin.0283.t
	desc = tarim_basin.0283.desc
	theme = RICE_theme_tarim_basin_town
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_zealous
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = tarim_basin.0283.a
		RICE_tarim_basin_bezeklik_pilgrimage_completed_log_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		# For Bokut's aspiration
		if = {
			limit = {
				root = character:302972
			}
			add_character_flag = RICE_bokut_did_bezeklik_pilgrimage
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:activity = {
				hidden_effect = { skip_activity_phase = yes }
			}
		}
	}


}
